 isaki vajah se gujarat or rajasthan main agle 24 ghante tak bahut baari barish kii ashanka bani hui he

 duusari taraf dakshini bangladesh or pashchim bengal ke gangey kshetron ke upar ek cychlonic sarkulation bana hua he

 santulan bananaa mushkil he kyonki khilaadi bhi insaan he

 hamale main saat logon kii maut ho gai he or 25 jakhmi shraddhalu ghayal ho gaye

 vaise amarnath yatriyon par yah pehla aantki hamalaa nahin he

 san 1993 main harakatul ansaar aatanki sanghathan ne amarnath yatriyon par hamale kiye the

 san 1994 main phir se harakatul ansaar ne yatriyon par hamalaa kiya
